name:V‚ÄçL‚ÄçA‚ÄçD‚ÄçY‚ÄçS‚ÄçL‚ÄçA‚ÄçV
info:DELUXE KING NON-SMOKING
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Couples
info:11 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted July 13, 2021
msg:Typical Chinese hotel.  We booked this hotel for 2 nights.  Calling in advance and clarifying whether the pool works, since, in principle, we were driving only for the sake of it.  We were told that the pool is open until 6 pm, and then there will be some kind of closed party, and we will have to leave, and the next day we can be in the pool until 11 pm.  In fact, when we arrived and checked in, we were told that due to the party, the pool was not allowed all day.  We were very upset as it was my birthday and we planned to relax by the pool until 6 pm, as the girl from the front desk told us on the phone.  For a long time we tried to find out why this happened, but no one could say anything concrete.  The woman at the reception just shrugged and sighed, how they love to do it.  They never brought us any fruit to the room, this is given the fact that it‚Äôs my birthday for a second and in normal hotels they always congratulate the guest (and a plate of fruit is, in principle, included in the price).  Further breakfasts.  Be prepared that breakfast costs more than 200 RMB and does not include coffee.  For coffee you need to pay extra 55 yuan per cup!  And finally the long-awaited pool.  We arrived at 10:05 right after opening.  The door was closed, no one was there, then we managed to find someone from the staff, we slowly opened the lock, let us into the pool area, as soon as we chose the sun loungers, the staff began to carry some furniture past us in the back, this  lasted about an hour, until I made a comment that this should be done before the arrival of the guests, before 10 am.  Moreover, it was possible to carry this furniture in a different path and not walk around our sun loungers all the time, dragging this furniture and talking loudly.  Further numbers.  We had a superior room, in which there was practically no refrigeration, everything else was new, albeit cheap.  It was very surprising that none of the staff for two and a half days never greeted us, neither at the pool, nor at the reception, nor at breakfast.  But, I want to mention one chef, he is the only one who greeted and tried to help and prepare scrambled eggs as we asked.  Everyone else didn‚Äôt give a damn, they just walked, looked, talked loudly, rubbed the plates and cutlery under our ear, until we again reprimanded them.  And on the last day I came to the pool at 10:15, to my surprise, the door was already open.  The girl was sitting on the edge, playing on the phone and did not even raise her head when I entered and sat on the lounger, until I called her and asked for a towel and a mattress for my lounger.  As a result, she did not know what kind of mattress I needed, called another guy, who also did not understand why I needed a mattress on a sunbed and where to get it.  He walked sighing, whining, until he brought me a mattress and just threw it on my lounger.  I was very upset when I found out that I would not be alone and I needed another mattress and another towel.  In general, if you do not take into account all the above facts and one lost day without a pool, I still managed to relax, but it was worth a lot of effort and wasted nerves.  The impression is that the staff does not understand at all that they are staff and why they are in this hotel.  The pool is large and spacious which is a plus.  But be prepared for the fact that there may be another party here that you will not be warned about and you, like me, will simply waste your time and money.  And the next day you will swim in the pool with glasses from the same party.
 Speaking of money, the room cost me over 700 RMB per night including breakfast (no coffee).  I think it is quite overstated, given all the negative factors.  Special thanks to the only caring employee of this hotel - the chef.  I wish the staff development and development again, and the owners, to reconsider the prices of rooms and coffee for breakfast, because there is no such price for coffee in any coffee shop in the city.

msg:The location of this hotel is relatively remote, near the Capital Airport. I found this hotel because of swimming. There are indoor and outdoor swimming pools. The summer vacation has begun, and I brought my daughter to swim for one night.

The hotel is very stylish. There is a large aquarium in the lobby. I thank Guo Ronghua and Liu Xuan at the front desk for sending small gifts and upgrading the original deluxe room to a business room. There is a small restaurant in the room, and the check-in process is also very good. quick. The business room is spacious and bright, larger than the general hotel room, and the air conditioning and water pressure are very powerful. The hotel's garage is very large, and anyone who turns in it will get lost, and it's free.

On summer weekends, there are many people in the indoor swimming pool. There are 4 swimming lanes in total, and 2 are allocated for teaching. There are more people in the outdoor swimming pool, and it is hard to find a reclining chair next to it. Many foreigners come in to enjoy the sun as soon as the door is opened, and they can bask in the sun all day. Therefore, it is recommended to come back to the outdoor swimming pool after 8 pm, there will be much fewer people and the loungers will not be so nervous.

The surrounding area of the hotel is relatively desolate, but you can order takeaway. If you take your children, you can go to the nearby Uwobao Family Growth Center and Bouncy Apes Super Sports Center, which are not far away. For dining and shopping, you can go to Sprys Outlet, Xiangyun Town.

Speaking of shortcomings, the hotel's buffet breakfast is average, there are fewer dishes to choose from, and I feel nothing to eat. The toilet in the guest room smelled bad at night, and it was fine the next day. The refrigerator in the room is locked and is said to be opened only for Ctrip guests. There is a lot of white hair in the outdoor pool, which is difficult to clean from the swimsuit. The ticket for the outdoor swimming pool is not included in the room rate and needs to be purchased in a package or separately. Unless you can go early to grab a lounger for a day, it will be difficult to get the ticket back.

Overall, this hotel meets the 4-star standard and is suitable for parent-child leisure.
